Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	If the swelling is on [the patient's] feet, the reduction will be easy and the alignment towards the mouth of the bladder will be easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a .i. drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it [the swelling] is narrow in the belly or thigh, then you must draw it out with one cloth wrap around the hand.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and cut open the belly or thigh, until the moisture that is there flows.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure,	And if other members are dislocated, and the head remains.
si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	If the nail of the thumb is struck deep into the wound of the wife, and it is pulled out until it reaches her mouth.
puis i boute .i. oncine ou ij., et le trai fuer;	Then insert one or two fingers, and pull forth.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier,	And if the wife's mouth is narrowed due to a hot abscess that has come, it is not necessary to force it.
ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	It is necessary to administer moist and fatty things;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	And apply plasters, and soften it in warm water and moistening agents.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the bone is on its surface, and you can make it even, apply what we have said in the previous step.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	And if there is no ability to do so, break it into pieces and leave nothing of the remaining tissue.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, bring him what we said in the dressing of abscesses that come to the marriage;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if bleeding occurs, let it be stopped with binding, and bring other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	I saw a woman in whom the fetus had died, then another was consulted on that case, and the death of the other fetus was prevented.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess came in the armpit and swelled so much that it burst open, and began to rot.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to treat it, and I thought for a long time, but could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a plaster of strong attraction, and an bone came out, and after some days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marveled greatly, for the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em miglior point;	I make the wound, and into it I insert bones, until the woman is better.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and the woman stays long in such a state, and then a little pus comes out from the place.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have never heard this chapter except because, when the master finds something strange, he knows what to do about it.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring the husband back to his place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	Here follows the shape of the lever, to which books are applied; and at two turns, the heads of the two links.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	The horns should be thinner than the restrictor, and made of ebony or boxwood.
et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the barrel of the pipe should be one finger's width wide, and the edges of the arms one finger-width, and of long a half palm.
et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	And between the two limbs should be two joints of the same bone, which are tightly joined in one and the other, half a palm length or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	And this pair of joints are pushed into the mouth of the jaw to open when turning the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, should be made of ebony or boxwood, according to the appearance of pliers.
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	And say to the two shoulders, as you see, of one span in length, and two fingers in width;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	And when you see to open the wife with all the tools, make her sit on one bed, her feet hanging and legs apart;
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	then push the two shoulders together in the woman, and hold the head of the tool beneath her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then work your hand with all the tools, just as you have done with pliers equally, according to the quantity that you see to open the mouth of the anvil, until the bail makes what it desires.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	These tools are all covered and have similar shapes; and when the smiths have equipped them, they work more quickly, and at a greater height for men because of their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not disdain the tool that you have not equipped, as its necessity is not easily excused.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second child is held back during birth, you must instruct the woman to retain her breath, and then make her vomit with discomfort, and hold your hands at her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	If she jumps because of this, it is good (or correct).
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If it is not so, take a small pot and make a poutice or cover and put herbs that can open the mouth of the woman, such as rue, anise, chamomile, cascara sagrada, and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	All these herbs, or some of them, should be cooked or boiled in water on the fire; then put a tube or pierced pot lid on the pot, and the other end into the mouth of the patient.
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	And hold the plaster until the vapor enters the patient's mouth; then make him vomit, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the second one suddenly moves quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	If it remains after this treatment and does not heal as expected, command the woman to moisten her left hand with oil of cumin or mustard plaster, and then put it on naturally.
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And she seeks the second joint; and when she has found it, if she takes it and stretches it little by little straightly, so that the husband does not resist during extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	but you must move it gently to the right and to the left, and then pull; if it comes and dislocates itself.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the husband's mouth is opened wide, we have said the cure of emptying and fumigating with herbs.
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if there is no such thing as we have said, make sure you do not pull too much.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	But it is necessary that the one at the mouth of the woman's womb, you tie him to the woman's thigh, then apply a clisterium ointment four-fold.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	If it is possible to retrieve and replace [the object], it will pass; but nonetheless, when she can do so, if a bad smell comes from the stomach and the head, it will poison the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	Therefore, necessary are suitable fumigations for this [case]: no ancient has proven the fumigation of dill and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman to retain flowers and secondary ones, is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it resembles glass in shape, with the head being thin in the nature and the large sides over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let the fumigation be over the coals, and let the tinder burn until it is consumed, then start another.
de percier lou fondement	to bore through the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have the foundation pierced, but it is stopped by some subtle means.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Then you must have the obstruction pierced with the correct tool, and not with a sharp splint, and ensure that it does not touch the flesh.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then put moist linen soaked in wine and oil on top of it, then treat with ointment until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will not come out again, place a plug of wood and leave it for several hours, and remove it when the child wants to go to bed in the room.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	And sometimes this sudden swelling of wound or abscess occurs; it must be covered. If it is inflamed, as we have said, the bandage of cloth should be used.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula from its base
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come from below the base are swellings, and those that come out of the sides of it, or in between the two parts,
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	If it has a fistula or more than one; and when the swelling is old, if it opens up, then add moisture to make it white or thin pus.
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And sometimes these fistulas are persistent; and they are known by those who have them or an evacuation or windy passage when the patient has an evacuation, and accidentally urinate in it.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And if the fistulas pierce up to the bladder and halfway down the penis; they reach up to the knee joint and the nut of the thigh.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one recognizes the fistula piercing through to its foundation, and not piercing entirely through:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	it is that you insert your index finger or foundation, and insert a fine needle of iron or steel into the fistula where there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	and if it has twisting, then insert a thin linen or horsehair tent, or hair, until you feel the tent or hair at your finger:
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	And if you do not feel it, neither pus nor putrid matter nor worm comes out, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	(Note: This line is a continuation of the previous one and I am translating both lines together in one English translation)
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	If the fistula is open all the way to the bladder or the conduit of urine, if it gushes out urine and cannot be sealed by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced all the way to the knee joint, then the tendon comes to the surface:   (Note: I have combined two lines into one translation as they are related)
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If it is not twisted and the source of pain is around, then it is indeed broken, and no medicine or ointment has any effect on it.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	In these Persian fistulas there is no cure but pain and futility of foolish physicians who interfere with it.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	In one that is not Persian and not old, in hope of healing by iron, as I have experienced,
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and it is that the patient lies between your hands on his back; and he lifts his legs up to his thighs, and has his thighs inclined towards his stomach.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then insert a tent of arrows, or of planks if there is curvature, as long as you know where the tent comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If the patient feels it around the foundation, then it is necessary that you insert your finger to indicate.
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	then you will know that the tent has penetrated; and it should be discovered where your finger feels the sore or the flesh, then you will know that it is pierced.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if it is not worked, it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One should say, however, that one can heal some, but it happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and help is given, if it is heating the fine cautery according to the width of the fistula, as has been said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and put everything hot in the fistula until it reaches the base; and do this 2 or 3 times, as long as you know that these charred fibers should be burned, which are similar to a feather of a bird;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	And then, cure the swollen tents with butter, until the heat subsides, then apply a soothing and healing ointment.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If it heals like this, that is good. But if it cannot be healed in any other way;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the tent enters but does not penetrate to the base, and between your finger and the tent, place a thick covering of fat or sycamore, and you see the fistula beneath the cover with care;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If the edge of the fistula begins, push it forward towards the opening, and then apply the cautery afterwards, until it reaches the head of the opening.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	When the opening is released and closed again, find those charred pieces that resemble a bird's feather, and nothing remains.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the flesh grows over it, cut between you and the wound, then cauterize it with fire or medicinal herbs.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For fire cauteries have two good effects: firstly, the removal of charred tissue around the wound, and secondly, stopping the flow of blood and drying up moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then heal the tents of wet cloths in butter or in boiled cheese, until the wounds are closed, and let the charred parts burn in the butter/cheese.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then heal the wound with hard charred medicine, and these are dry medications.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it heals and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	If a fistula comes to the full extent of its foundation and is removed from the body, push your thumb or finger into it and examine it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel the tension and between two is the cloth or the linen or leather, or it is close to being pierced, there should not be any other way than a faith and hope-giving method through the administration of one of the three ways:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have said, or you strike it to the bottom, or if you boil it, then treat it as we have described before.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep that you cover the holding element for the foundation, let the effusions come out through it voluntarily.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	Then heal (it), as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	In case it becomes healthy (the wound), then remove that covering and clean it when it is cut away from the base, either by tenting or using another instrument.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then disinfect the charred flesh that is in the wound, as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	Then study to heal the wound and to retain the fistula on the side farther from the base; it will be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And sometimes they are fistulas in this manner: and it is when you bite the tip into the fistula, and it is where it touches the foundation beneath the skin above.
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and take a piece of parchment pierced at its head in this shape:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	and put one twisted thread through two, and push the parchment along with the whole thread into the fistula until it reaches the head.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it [the joint] is dislocated at the margin of the foundation within, then extract the thread of that one, so you pierce your finger or foundation.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	and draw out the head of the thread, and bring together the two shoulder blades, and hold one against the other, and leave it for 1 or 2 days.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and keep it immobile until the threads meet the bones that are between them, and become joined.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then heal the wound until it is healed and healthy.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not pierce itself, make it pierce in all possible ways, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For you should not treat the fistula too deeply by cauterizing it, and then heal it as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spur-like spathulum used to make a fistula is very sharp at one end and slices.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on the other hand, not because one should not strike what one should not copy, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Hemorrhoids are of two kinds: either they are within the foundation, like a piece of resin, and there are both small and large ones; and in the skin, blood flows out immediately.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	and there is one or more of them, they are outside the foundation and at the head of the foundation; but those that are outside have little moisture,
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	And always or a little of sour lemon juice or a little blood, and it has the color of the body.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment for those with it within their foundations, since you instruct the patient to strain for urination in rooms, until the foundations pass, and this appears in the sons.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	hasten it, and pierce it with pincers or hold it with your nail, then strike at its roots;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the hinges cannot be held by their moisture, take a small cloth or cotton, or a piece of camel's hair;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	And draw them to your hands, then strike them, and pour some hot powders upon them that serve as a substitute for cautery.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you cauterize them as described in the "cautery" chapter, then treat them with other remedies until they are healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the foundation cannot be removed, clisterize the patient with biting and harsh cleansers to cleanse the area where the foundation is located, so that it can come out easily.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	If the patient applies oil to himself, and his hairs are deeply rooted in the foundation, then the treatment is easy;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And it is that you grasp them with your nail or tweezers, strike them, then heal them as we have said, until they are healed and fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	You should make the stitch in this way: take a twisted thread and put it on a needle, then pull the thread above and pierce the needle from the other side, and twist the two threads below the needle.
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and if it is wide, make the stitch tight, then knot the thread, pull out the needle, and do the same with all the others, leaving one for the blood flow.
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place a soft cloth soaked in rose oil or wax on the foundation, and place it, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then let it drain until it stops, and when it is dried, heal it with ointment and other treatment, until it heals.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	With the fire or foundation.
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Often there is drying of feces in the intestines due to natural constriction, and when the illness is old and medicine is not helpful.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary for you to peel the skin at the tip of a splinter or your fingernail, so that it does not get wet.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then heal it until it heals as required;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it cannot heal, then repeat the shaving more forcefully until it heals, and be peeled;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then heal it until it is healed.
dou fremit	The trembling (or shuddering)
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Louse is a small pustule appearing before the body, and it travels throughout;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And sometimes the troutworm freezes (or paralyzes), and it is felt like death trembling throughout the body, and more in the hands than other parts.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the remedy is that you take a cane from an ostrich feather or a strong goose feather and place it on the trembling (patient), until the circles contract the trembling completely;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand along the entire cane until you cover the trembling entirely and push it into completely, and strengthen the trembling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see, do this with a cane of iron or steel following this form and be subtle underneath and train above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	Do not pierce [the area], for it should be held by the thumb, and it should be pressed. And if you wish, cauterize the trembling, as described in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	The form of the clyster (enema) is   ...
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Never is an enema made with silver or iron, or melted tallow or resin; and at times, small and large instruments are made according to those for whom they are prepared.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, those whom one treats in the care of children and who are weak and painful, are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the cupping glass is both small and large, or the belly is tied in this manner:   (This seems to describe a tool used for cupping therapy.)
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	and it has an opening or the belly is tied, as you see, and the cheeks are pierced within; and at one side there are two holes, and in the other one.  (This seems to describe a design for the cupping glass.)
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	And let the stomach or man put the medicine from a beast's bladder or parchment, and it should be pierced all around with small holes.
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And at each hole there should be space of one inch, then push in each hole a strong thread of twisted cord in ten or fewer, and bind the stomach like a goat's pouch.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And when the medicine is inside, tie it with a strong thread to the instrument in front, then smear (clisterize). This is the shape of a circle.
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the clistere with oil or egg yolk, or something similar, then insert it gently.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	Then the ministers stretch out the patient's two hands together while he is completely visible, then remove the cloth, and wash the patient's legs at the surface.
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	If the medication seems to come out, squeeze it as much as possible; and if it does not go away all at once, letting it stay for an entire night increases its benefit.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	If you treat the patient with a cloth for the disease of abdominal distention, and the medication seems to come out quickly, continue it until he is cured.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are fleshy or abscessed, it should be cleansed as gently as for an infant;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the gentle cleanse where the skin is stretched:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have said in the division the treatment for wounds; now we will tell you about hand treatments and medicines, according to their completion.  --> We have already mentioned the cure for wounds in the previous division; now we will tell you about hand treatments and medicines according to the process or method.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and of what kind they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things that cause wounds are by piercing with a spear, cutting with a sword and knife, or lance, mace or arrow, or similar things.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or according to the parts of the body, such as a wound that falls on the neck, head, chest, abdomen, liver, and similar limbs.
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you the treatment for every wound, and I shall begin with the simple wounds of the head, because it will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	And if it is a simple wound of the head and the bone is not broken, be careful that it is from an arrow or similar things, and the skin is torn all the way through and the wound is large.
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and you doubt raising an abscess hot: if you do so immediately, clean the head wound itself whether it comes a little blood from the wound or opposite of the injured part.
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	And the patient should evacuate himself of wine and large meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	If he does not want to purge (sainier), his food should be reduced, and he should not drink wine, nor eat meat.
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And apply on the wound, if an abscess comes out, cotton wool soaked in rose oil or in vinegar steeped.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	If there is no abscess, then apply on the wound if it is fresh with all its blood, and it has not been moved by air, here is a little powder that I will say later.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the arrow has moved it, then apply some ointments until it heals.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	If the wound is large like that of a sword and similar, and the lips cannot be brought together by pressure, then stitch it up, as I will say for belly wounds, with sewing.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound exposes the bone and pus, but only holds together by a little, press it; then heal the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh instead of skin.
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	And instruct the patient to eat coarse foods such as boiled heads (testes) and wheat, also including peas and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find or suspect rotten flesh not on the bone, press it all and throw away the pus, then heal it.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein without a cord, and it cannot be stopped by medicine, then tie it, and if you find it dislocated, bind it with a thread;
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if that does not help, cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, the cure is easy: you put in this powder which hardens as soon as the astringent has set it;
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the method of the powder is: take one part of incense; two parts of dragon's blood; three parts of quicklime, and grind them finely together,
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	apply the wound, and press it firmly until it drains well and joins all its blood.
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	and then bind it tightly and leave it to heal, if it does not swell; for the medicine is not removed until it has healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And sometimes this is done with quicklime only when there is no incense or dragon's blood, but the sore has not moved.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the wound has moved, most certainly do not put this powder on it;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but place some digested herbs or wheat flour made with water and honey on it until it swells.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then cure it with other remedies until it is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	and if the bone fracture comes with the wound and it is small, extract it using fine pliers.
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	And I will tell you after this about the breaks of the head.
de la plaie dou col	about the wound of the neck   (neck injury)
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If a wound occurs in the neck and it is simple, without any difference between it and that of the head, but if the nerve or the artery is cut.  (neck injury with damage to nerves/artery)
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the nerve, there is no other remedy than to let it heal and not put anything binding, for it harms nerves and makes them shrink;
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And do not put anything cold on the wound, for the substance of nerves is cold, and their continuation is with the brain, which is the highest member.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	but let the medicine be warm, such as warm water washed with mild soap, and mixed with rose oil, and also cooked in warm water.
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other stones of similar manner, and always moist.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, bind it with a bandage, then treat until it heals.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and swollen with pus, pierce or dig lower.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the arteries are cut and bleeding occurs, stop it, ligate it, and cauterize as needed;
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	and if the spine of the throat is cut or the veins are severed, keep them closed so that the meat remains.
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	tie up the vein above the throat of the neck, and do not touch the throat but place it back in its natural position;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then apply the traction method, and leave it for some days, then cure it with hot compresses until it heals.
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	If the wound presses on the bone, break it.
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	If there are pieces of bone, pull them out if you can, and those that you cannot remove, leave until the wound festers.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	And let the joint be dislocated and aligned.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, sprinkle on it the powder that I have said.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	If there is bone in the wound and it has a fistula, then cure it as I have said in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of the wound from a spear or knife.
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a wound from a lance or knife, and the wound is deep, look to see if bubbles rise from the wound; therefore, know that the wound is deadly.
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it is not deep, and the wound is fresh with all its blood, do not put powder on it at first hour or bind it for the blood that causes it to swell.
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	return to the patient's heart and kill him;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	But apply an attracting ointment, and let it lie for two times per day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	And if you don't have ointment, put in the wound old cotton to draw out moisture.
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	and let the patient sleep on the wound for three days, or four, or more.
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if no spasm, nor evil tremor of heart, nor drawing of bowels with entrail does not occur;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	And when you see the good positioning, know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat it with poultices and other cures, as long as it is healthy;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	If it cannot heal, then open it, know that there is a fistula; cure it accordingly.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	If the wound is from a sword or knife cut and it is simple (not complex), then cure the part that is in front;
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	If it is large, stitch it up; and if it is small, powder it, and if it has been pressed into the bone, take away pieces of it, be it a wound, and pull out the threads if they are drawn.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	And if they are not drawn, let the wound fester, align the extraction.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	and for other wounds on other limbs, it is the judgement as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	The breakage of the stomach
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The rupture of the stomach is great, medium, and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	A large wound makes the intestines or the nerves of the intestines protrude once in a while through it.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	And stitching is more difficult, and sometimes a small wound is worth more than a large one,
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	because when one puts more points in (the body), if one does not put them in from end to end;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	because the intestines swell soon enough that they feel the cold, if they are pushed more inwards,
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	And because it is more important to heal the midline wounds, because one rearranges the intestines back into their place for them rather than for others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And know that the wound of the belly is in four ways:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	The two common wounds occur in the abdominal wound,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	And the suturing of other wounds on the body, as well as two other specific suturings, are common to other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	Moreover, they are more appropriate with the suturing of the belly, and I will explain one and then the other.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and nothing from the intestines is protruding,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	And a third thing is about resetting, which can be done in one of two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	For the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	For because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, heat it up in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	soak a sponge or a piece of fine linen in warm water only,
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	Or you cook in hot water with squill (squinant) and cypress (cipre) and thorn (spike).
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	And soften the intestine until the inflammation is removed.
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And sometimes make this wine restraining, and it's good to soothe what swells for reduction of inflammation.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the inflammation spreading, if there is a raw intestine or a bad intestine that has been cooked,
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	Because this narrows the entrance to little things;
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if it cannot enter, make a small incision with the instrument used for hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	and the first cure is to grind the root;
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	we should not cut it unnecessarily.
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	And this is the instrument to split:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	slice within along the curvature and do not bend it, and observe its shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is widened, and the intestines escape:
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	If you reset it according to its natural form in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	If you have the power, for it is necessary. (Note: The "car" here implies that the action of resetting is necessary, but not that the patient or someone else has the ability to do so.)
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is wide and it is in the part below the belly,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	you must make the patient lie on his back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	And raise his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	If it is in the part beneath the belly,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	If he raises his head and his feet higher than the parts beneath:
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and if the rupture of the belly is in one of the two parts:
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	If the broken part is higher than the other.
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus it is necessary to treat as I say in large and small wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	In small wounds, use what is appropriate.
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	Then place a skilled and compassionate minister between your hands who will treat the entire wound with his hand,
et assemble les levres;	And gather the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common method of suturing.
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and you take one needle or more, according to the width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	Then leave one inch of space from the edge of the wound and stitch with a needle having one strong thread.
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	And pierce the two shoulders with the two sharp bones (of a splint or instrument).
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is beneath the skin within, as far as you make it penetrate that part.
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and assemble the two shoulders of the splint in four.
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then draw a double thread around the needle of two parts (i.e., twice),
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	Then assemble the two shoulders of the wound properly.
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	And leave one finger space, and insert another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then tie the thread as you did for the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and do not stop doing this according to what you have need of the needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until the entire wound is constricted;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	and the needles be medium-sized, between thin and thick.
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because fine needles pierce all the flesh, while very thick ones cannot enter well.
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	Because they should be cut open;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and it is not advisable to push the needles too deep into the flesh and skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	so that they do not open and cut the wound before the joint;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	then pierce the head of the needles, so that it does not hurt the patient while sleeping,
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	And place bands or cloths on the head of the arrows to keep them still,
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and let them remain until the wound is healed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	and this method of stitching arrows is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because it takes one or two arrows to do it.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second stitch is common.
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and you assemble the two shoulders of the hide and the two shoulders of the sack together with a needle having one strong, medium thread.
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	and when you have sewn these four pieces together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	if you unravel the needle at the part where you began, in the way that cloaks are sewn.
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	And place a distance between each stitch the thickness of a small egg.
ceste costure sevent li home,	this stitching should be for the man.
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	and I sew a wound on the belly of a man.
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	who was wounded by a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound is more than one palm long,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and protrudes from the abdomen about two palms in length,
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	and was located within the belly,
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I brought back the intestines when it had been twenty-four hours.
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	and the wound healed up to fifteen days, and it was cured, and became healthy.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they had judged him that he would die, but this was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and I did not cure it with medicine, because at that time there was none available nor any medicines;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	And apply old cotton above the wound twice a day, and wash it with honey water until it heals.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	I will tell you the two proper methods of stitching:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle and thread from the outside to the inside part.
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	when it has passed through the core straight, if you find that the knot or stitch where you put the needle,
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	And make it pierce from the other side through the inner part up to where it protrudes.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	and the understanding of this stitch is that you sew as the pilgrims sew fur,
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	and that you leave the seam once on one side, and take it up from the other, until the stitch is completely finished.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of stitching, which Galen calls specifically,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	is as anyone does who joins two parts naturally together,
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and apply one of the ends of the thread to the other end, in this manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	insert an awl or the nearest thread end and pierce only that spot,
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	And let the two cheeks (or sides) remain open;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	Then turn the needle and make it pierce from the outer part to the inside.
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	with both cheeks (or sides) open;
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	Then pierce one and the other from the outer part to the inside, in two other cheeks (or sides) that are opposite each other.
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	And this is the common method of stitching (or sewing).
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen said this word, and no one denies it.
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	One should sew the stomach with two needles, each having thread in it.
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and one should thrust one needle from one side, and the other from the other side, in the manner of those who sew corsets.
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	And know that when the hernia is within the abdomen,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	is the stitching more severe than in other parts of the belly.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgments for the wound are as follows for other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	And it is when you find the fresh wound full of blood, as soon as the arrows have moved it,
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	then insert the arrow and tie it; then put powder rejuvenating flesh on top.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	if the arrow has moved it, then put some ointment on it that is present, until the wound heals;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and sew the flesh with thread, and bind the strips of linen cloth;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat the wound as others, while it is healthy;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	and if you have no medicine, put on it (the wound) as soon as it starts to discharge pus, old cotton.
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and move it two times a day while it is healthy.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you have no need for other medicines in many cases where the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	And if you doubt whether the wound will infect the main limbs,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	then wet a thin cloth lightly in warm oil or rose oil.
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	then wrap it around the joints, and beneath the bones;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	And if pain or swelling occurs in the belly, and it often happens,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	and if the clysters of black wine make it hot, and particularly when the swelling reaches the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	and pierce inside, and know that when it is the large intestine, it is easier to heal than the small.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine called "jeun" cannot heal when it is perforated,
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	And it is due to the planting of veins that they are, and because of the subtlety of all the body, and the proximity of its nature to nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the worm jumps out from the wound, return it back like the intestines, while it is still fresh.
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	and if it is old and has turned into or black, you must cauterize the blackened part where blood does not flow from it.
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	because there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	Then grip what is between the ligament,
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	and place the two shoulders hanging from the part below the wound towards the side to align the extraction when the arrow falls out, and the wound bows.
de la routure dou boueil	of the boil's rupture
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are torn, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	if it can be restored in some men,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	because I have seen a man pierced or gutted by a spear;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	And it became ulcerated and turned into a fistula, and from this came the discharge and windiness;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I applied remedy according to what I know, and did not stop refining it until it was healed, and the wounds sealed.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw the wound sealing, I feared that the patient had something wrong in his stomach;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	but he was not ill, but remained in better condition, and diet and drink;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	And they said to any experimenters that when there is a small wound in the intestine, it should be tied in this manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take large thongs, then bring together the lips of the wound,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	and when the thongs have opened the mouth, place it on the two lips,
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	so that it stretches its mouth above;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	And then grip the head (of the patient), and hold it so that it cannot dislocate.
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	Then put another force after in the same manner as before, until the wound is completely grasped;
et cout la plaie.	and stitch the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	If the head (abscess) abscesses in the intestines, it causes no harm to the patient.
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	And it can be tied with a fine thread that is cut from the intestine of an animal.
en teil maniere:	in this manner:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	take the head of this thread made of intestine which should be quite thin.
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	then tie the head of this thread (the intestine thread) with a fine linen cord twisted around it.
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	Then insert the thread into the needle, sew the intestine, and reset it in the wound.
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	And this way of suturing wounds is not beyond faith and hope.
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	And if the wound is large and wide, especially when it is in one of the small intestines, there is no remedy or healing, except through subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	from a fistula or...
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	Know that every wound or abscess, when it heals, is universally called "fistula."
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	and likewise when it is closed and healed.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	And a fistula is according to the truth, a swelling lasting long and white, where there is no pain.
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	and is as swollen as the feathers of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	And sometimes in a clear jump, and other times thick;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	Sometimes shallow, and other times deep;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	And I have spoken about it in the section on wounds, that every wound that is not healed, and there is no flesh,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	It is not only due to one of the eight causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	It means, "This is to know, by the smallness of blood or heart;"
ou por sa malice;	And by its badness;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	Or because there is hard flesh within, under the lips, which does not allow flesh to grow;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	or it has too much pus;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	If the loosened joint is of bad quality matter, then [the following action is advised]:
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	and the medicine is not good in treating it;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	because corruption is a type of pestilence.
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	Because the property in that region causes slow digestion, and slows health, and naturally decays by nature;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	There are veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	And I have already shown all these causes, and the signs, and the treatments of medicines in the divisions:
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	And I will tell you how to treat a fistula made by manual work:
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Recall that fistula occurs in all members of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	for there are fistulas that come from large veins, and arteries, and nerves,
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or in the intestines, or the bladder, or one of the ribs,
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	or in the spine of the back, or any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	And if it comes to the property of the principal member, and similar limbs.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all the fistulas that are made in this way are difficult healing, and there is nothing but labor and ignorance.
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	And if there is any fistula that does not reach the level I have said, and you are confident of its cure,
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	And you shall recognize it (the dislocation), if you take a tent of beeswax or iron, if the fistula is straight, then insert it.
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	and if the fistula is twisted, then search for a slender tent reed.
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	because reeds bend easily due to twisting.
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	and if the fistula is crushed in many places and you cannot search for it well with reeds,
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	If the clisterization is performed by one of the wounds,
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	for the moisture cuts from one wound to another, and it purifies.
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	then you shall cauterize it as best you can, knowing if there is bone or nerve, and it is filled up to the full.
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	and ask the patient carefully about the pain he feels when pressed by your hand, and where he feels it.
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	And when you truly know the place where it is located, and if it is far from a joint, or a nerve, or an artery, or a vein,
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	or in any of the places that I have told you, if it is turned as I have said,
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and cut open the cavity and the rotten and corrupt matter within;
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	and then heal it until it is healed,
et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	And if the fistula is properly deepened correctly, then you must stop it up, as much as you can.
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	Then put moistened tents in healing balm and push them into the head of the fistula,
tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	until the medicine corrodes the excess that remains at the bottom;
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then put salves with healing balm on it until it heals.
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	If not healed by this means, then cauterize as we have said.
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	and if the bone is corrupted from the fistula, crush it.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If vein or nerve does not trouble you or main limbs as we have said.
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee,	And if the bone is exposed, and there is corruption and blackness, leave it to fester until all the corruption is removed,
puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	then heal with healing herbs until it is healed.
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant,	and if not healed, then let it swell as before,
saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	know that you are not to wait until the fountain (source of water).
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons,	If you dig deep and wish to be at the bottom,
et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	and remove all corruption, then return it to its place;
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	And if it is in such a state, that is good.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	If this is not the case, know that the corruption is too deep, you cannot reach it;
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	If there is no other remedy but to rest with natural means;
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles,	and if a small bone is corrupt, and you can draw it out with pliers;
si l’estrai a .i. estrument covenauble a ceu,	If it needs to be extracted using one instrument;
et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	if there are many bones, extract them all, not leaving any one behind;
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour,	and if the moisture opposes it and there is no error or fear,
si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	if it softens and moisten the bone and releases the bones.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture,	And if you cannot remove them within an hour, put on the wound something stimulating purgative.
et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os,	and let it remain until the flesh is rotten around the bones,
et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	And then if they have more easily movable bones;
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse,	and if it is a large bone like the thigh or shin:
si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee,	only remove the corruption until all the blackness is removed,
puis restoure la plaie;	then restore the wound;
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	And if there is a large part of corruption reaching to the bone.
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	It must be covered completely up to the corruption and then be healed until it is closed.
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint .i. home en sa jambe,	And I will tell you of a fistula that happened to one man in his leg.
si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	so that you may take example and aid in your work.
Il fut .i. jovencelz entor .xxx. ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors,	A young man of about 30 years had a pain in his leg due to a cause that came from within the body.
tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	until substances came to the leg, and there developed a large abscess without any cause for opening.
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri,	but they opened it further due to their foolishness, opening more abscesses.
et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	And it becomes full of matter, and a fistula forms, and much pus comes out that all are going bowel and moisture from the body.
et maint mire i mirent cure entor .ij. ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains,	And they put many remedies around it for two years, but there was no experienced person in the art of hands.
tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit,	as long as I was there, and I saw her leg and the medicines with which she was treated,
et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	and that was coming out through the sores with great effort.
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	And the youth's body becomes red, and has a yellowish color.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus,	I pitched a tent in one of the wounds, then I searched all the wounds.
et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	and found that one wound was coming towards the other from all parts of the leg.
